# Habitable conversion from the vanilla classes which spawn based on orbit distance will be based mostly on the temperature modifier
# Planets with the prescripted_ideal flag may result in any class which has @Perfect habitability value (seen in the species_traits_habitability file) related to the original class
# ie: A Chlorogenian homeworld will result in the neighbour ideal guaranteed world to spawn as chlorogenian too, which may get converted to Myciliogenian, Photogenian, Retinalgenian, or stay Chlorogenian
# Remaining uncolonized habitable worlds will all use the same conversion formula based on the temperature modifier, so its perfectly possible a Cryogenian can get converted to an Erimosthalassic
# The first function only handles habitable conversion to Terrestrial, Sub-terrestrial and Oceanic classes. The remaining types will be converted from uninhabitables in a different function

convert_habitable_class = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_planet_class = pc_continental } #Chlorogenian
		# Guaranteed confortable neighbours
		if = {
			limit = { has_planet_flag = "prescripted_ideal" }
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					change_pc = "orbit_chlorogenian"
					# Atmosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-optimal"
						days = -1
					}
					# Biosphere modifier
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							add_modifier = {
								modifier = "biosphere-sparse"
								days = -1
							}
							modifier  = { factor = 10 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
						}
						1 = {
							add_modifier = {
								modifier = "biosphere-diverse"
								days = -1
							}
							modifier  = { factor = 2 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
						}
						1 = {
							add_modifier = {
								modifier = "biosphere-dense"
								days = -1
							}
							modifier  = { factor = 10 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
						}
					}
					# Hydrosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "hydrosphere-water_abundant"
						days = -1
					}
					# Spawn gravity modifier
					spawn_gravity_modifier = yes
					update_portrait = yes
					set_planet_flag = "modifiers_spawned"
					set_planet_flag = "planet_converted"

					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
				}
				10 = {
					change_pc = "orbit_retinalgenian"
					# Atmosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-optimal"
						days = -1
					}
					# Biosphere modifier
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							add_modifier = {
								modifier = "biosphere-sparse"
								days = -1
							}
							modifier  = { factor = 10 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
						}
						1 = {
							add_modifier = {
								modifier = "biosphere-diverse"
								days = -1
							}
							modifier  = { factor = 10 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
						}
					}
					# Hydrosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "hydrosphere-water_abundant"
						days = -1
					}
					# Spawn gravity modifier
					spawn_gravity_modifier = yes
					update_portrait = yes
					set_planet_flag = "modifiers_spawned"
					set_planet_flag = "planet_converted"

					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
				}
				10 = {
					change_pc = "orbit_photogenian"
					# Atmosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-optimal"
						days = -1
					}
					# Biosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "biosphere-diverse"
						days = -1
					}
					# Hydrosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "hydrosphere-water_dark"
						days = -1
					}
					# Spawn gravity modifier
					spawn_gravity_modifier = yes
					update_portrait = yes
					set_planet_flag = "modifiers_spawned"
					set_planet_flag = "planet_converted"

					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
				}
				10 = {
					change_pc = "orbit_myciliogenian"
					# Atmosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-optimal"
						days = -1
					}
					# Biosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "biosphere-sparse"
						days = -1
					}
					# Hydrosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "hydrosphere-water_abundant"
						days = -1
					}
					# Spawn gravity modifier
					spawn_gravity_modifier = yes
					update_portrait = yes
					set_planet_flag = "modifiers_spawned"
					set_planet_flag = "planet_converted"

					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
				}
			}
		}
		# Remaining
		else = {
			# Atmosphere modifier
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 13 }
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size < 16 }
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 20 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 10.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 10.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-toxic"
						days = -1
					}
				}
				5 = {
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 18 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 21 }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-marginal"
						days = -1
					}
				}
				3 = {
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size < 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-optimal"
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
			# Convert planet class based solely on temperature and atmosphere modifiers, as well as planet size (Terrestrials require optimal size from 17 to 22)
			random_list = {
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_ammoniagenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_chlorogenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_cryogenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_myciliogenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_photogenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_retinalgenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_thermogenian
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_archipelagic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_panthalassic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_cryopelagic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_thermopelagic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_panpelagic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 0  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_tropicothalassic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.75 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.25 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_thermothalassic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_cryothalassic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.75 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.25 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_megachloridal
					modifier  = { add = 15  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }

					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }

				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_alpicothalassic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.75 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.25 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.50 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					change_pc = orbit_erimosthalassic
					modifier  = { add = 5  planet_size > 16 planet_size < 23 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size < 17 }
					modifier  = { add = 10  planet_size > 22 }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.25 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.50 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }

			}
			# Biosphere modifier
			random_list = {
				0 = {
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "biosphere-barren"
						days = -1
					}
					modifier  = { add = 0  is_planet_class = orbit_ammoniagenian }
					modifier  = { add = 0  is_planet_class = orbit_chlorogenian }
					modifier  = { add = 10  is_planet_class = orbit_cryogenian }
					modifier  = { add = 0  is_planet_class = orbit_myciliogenian }

					modifier  = { add = 0  is_planet_class = orbit_retinalgenian }

					modifier  = { add = 0  is_planet_class = orbit_panthalassic }
					modifier  = { add = 10  is_planet_class = orbit_cryopelagic }

					modifier  = { add = 0  is_planet_class = orbit_megachloridal }
					modifier  = { add = 10  is_planet_class = orbit_alpicothalassic }
					modifier  = { add = 10  is_planet_class = orbit_erimosthalassic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.75 has_modifier = atmosphere-toxic }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = atmosphere-marginal }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.25 has_modifier = atmosphere-optimal }
				}
				0 = {
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "biosphere-sparse"

					update_portrait = yes
					set_planet_flag = "modifiers_spawned"
					set_planet_flag = "planet_converted"

					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
				}
				10 = {
					change_pc = "orbit_erimosthalassic"
					# Atmosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "atmosphere-optimal"
						days = -1
					}
					# Biosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "biosphere-sparse"
						days = -1
					}
					# Hydrosphere modifier
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "hydrosphere-water_limited"
						days = -1
					}
					# Spawn gravity modifier
					spawn_gravity_modifier = yes
					update_portrait = yes
					set_planet_flag = "modifiers_spawned"
					set_planet_flag = "planet_converted"

					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-scorching }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-hot }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-temperate }
					modifier  = { factor = 1.00 has_modifier = temperature-cold }
					modifier  = { factor = 0.00 has_modifier = temperature-freezing }
				}
			}
		}
	}
			
}
